<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">"<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[7-8].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">"<b>Preface</b>"<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>[11]<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>"Although I have spent a great
portion of my life studying religion in its various forms, I was not excited
about the prospect of undertaking a critical evaluation of the <b>Judeo-Christian
</b>[to me (LS) a loathsome term]<b> tradition</b>â€”for two reasons.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>First, with the resurgence of Christian
fundamentalism, it did not seem to be a particularly propitious time to write a
book questioning the validity and value of that tradition.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>And second, it has been my experience that <b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">any serious attempt to discuss the subject of
religion or philosophy leaves most people either infuriated or bored to death.<o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Nevertheless, after due reflection,
I concluded that precisely <b>because fundamentalism is so pervasive, there was
sufficient reason</b> <b>once again to <o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">566<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">________________________________________________________________<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always">
</span>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">expose
the dark side of the Judeo-Christian tradition.</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Not that it
hasn't been done many times before but, for reasons that I'll take pains to
explain, the true history of Western religions is constantly being swept aside
in favor of more expeditious myths.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><b>The second problemâ€”namely,
writing on religion in a style that would be sufficiently entertaining to hold
a reader's interest</b>â€”I found even more perplexing.<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>What reader would be encouraged to take the journey with me into
the oftentimes<b> labyrinthine world of theology and philosophy</b>?<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Surely not those zealots who are so
committed to their religious beliefs that even an examination of their belief
systems is considered sacrilegious.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>No
amount of reason or logic could persuade them.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>However, there does appear to be a large number of people who are not
committed to suppressing their intellectual integrity in blind adherence to an
unexamined system of beliefs.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>This is
especially true of many (although, sadly, not nearly enough) college students
who have adopted their religious views without being aware of the large body of
historical research that calls into question the motivations and integrity of
the founders of many of the popular religions of our time.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Few are aware of the origins of the biblical
writings, or have devoted any time to critically evaluating the messages that
such works convey.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>I find this to be
especially true of those who are able to quote passages of the Bible to suit
every occasion.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Even college students who have taken
courses in theology have often been denied exposure to the cogent arguments
that question the divinity of Jesus or the concept of a divine creator.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Worse still, disingenuous theology
professors often provide an atheistic strawman which can be easily disposed of
without coming to grips with the real contradictions of theism.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>I experienced this sort of ruse firsthand in
the theology and philosophy courses I took in college.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Virtually every serious philosopher who
questioned Christian metaphysics was given short shrift.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>It wasn't until after I left the university
that I was able to begin my real education.</b>"<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>[12].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>"Some may be offended by my
treatment of their deeply revered beliefs.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span><b>It is not my intention to offend or to destroy the psychological
comfort which belief in God and immortality offers to many persons</b> [but!,
it is one by-product]<b>.</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Rather, I
hope to forcefully demonstrate that beliefs which are thousands of years old,
and stem from an age when humankind was by and large ignorant and savage, need
to be carefully scrutinized for validity and relevance in today's society.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>If we are to formulate a sound ethic and
just and effective socioeconomic policies, we must, wherever possible, remove
all myths and falsehoods embedded in our theories.<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>I hope to create sufficient doubts regarding religious beliefs
that people will pause before attempting to translate <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">567<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">________________________________________________________________<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always">
</span>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">their
theological doctrines into public policy.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>As I will amply demonstrate, <b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">it
is the true believers, who attempt to back their beliefs with the power of the
state, who have caused so much misery throughout history.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Doubt encourages tolerance.<o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Given this rationale, I ask the
reader to accompany me on a mental excursion, back through the accumulated
religious traditions of Western society.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>The trip won't always be easy; for some it may become too painful to
continue.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>It is extremely
difficultâ€”some would argue impossibleâ€”to discard beliefs which have been
learned from parents and which are woven into the fabric of our culture.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Yet <b>the further progress of our society
requires that we perceive as clearly as possible the reality of the world as it
actually exists, rather than a world of myths, no matter how intoxicating those
myths may be. </b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</span>In the long run,
history has shown that intellectual hallucinogens will wreak havoc with any
society.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>The purpose of this volume is
to clear away the sediment of thousands of years of myths and deliberate
falsehoods in an effort to reach a bedrock of truth regarding <b>Western
society's Judeo-Christian beliefs.</b>"<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>[13].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">'<b>16<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">The Origins of Religion:<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">In the Beginning There Was Ignorance<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:2">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="mso-tab-count:
1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Shabriri,
briri, riri, iri, ri.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:2">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="mso-tab-count:
2">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>â€”Judaic chant to ward off demons<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">Religion
is easily stripped of its claim to a supernatural origin when examined from a
naturalistic perspective.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>In this
chapter and the next I'll show that <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial;
text-transform:uppercase">the origins of religion can be traced to the
fundamental psychological traits of humankind. </span></b><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">Some
of the most basic are:<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.25in;text-indent:-.25in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:
&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;"><span style="mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;">â€”</span></span><span style="font-family:Arial"> <span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>the need to
explain natural phenomena such as birth and death, sunrise and sunset, fire and
rain, the changing seasons, sickness and insanity, unusual geological
formations and even the origin of humankind;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.25in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.25in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:.5in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial">â€”<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">the desire to control
nature rather than be a helpless victim of impersonal forces;<span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">568<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">________________________________________________________________<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always">
</span>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.25in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:.5in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial">â€”<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">the desire of some
persons to control others through manipulation of basic fears and
superstitions; and<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.25in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:.5in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial">â€”<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">the usefulness of
religion for developing social adhesion and control.'<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>[367].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.25in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.25in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">'<b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">Using Immortality to Sell Christianity<o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">A
new theology of itself would have been tough to sell had Paul not had in
reserve the ultimate elixir of the patent medicine tradeâ€”immortalityâ€”guaranteed
to all who believed in his god.</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Now, this was really something!<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Kings and heroes always had the chance of
making the leap to immortality with the gods.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>But for the poor peons at the bottom of the social heapâ€”who were the
majority in those daysâ€”the best one could hope for was to end up as a vague
"shade" wondering [I expected:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>wandering] in Sheol (Hades).<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>The
Christian concept of heaven, on the other hand, was pure bliss.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>When the Greek philosopher Celsus
criticized Christianity as blind faith, he was undoubtedly right; but what
appealing alternative did he have to offer?<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>Only an inglorious end after a life of suffering.</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Today many thousands commit suicide every
year and risk eternal damnation just to end their wretched lives.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Is it any wonder that two thousand years ago
many equally desperate people would soon be willing to throw down their
miserable lives in order to attain eternal happiness?<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>After all, <b>there have never been any complaints from
disillusioned martyrs.<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>The promise of heaven was recognized
for its military value even before the dawn of Christianity.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>Julius Caesar wrote that the Druids
believed "the cardinal doctrine that souls do not die, but after death
pass from one to another and this belief, casting fear of death aside, they
hold to be a great incentive of valor.</b>"<sup>18</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Originally, the Judaic idea of an afterlife
was similar to that of the ancient Greeks.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>One fate awaited all:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>after
death they existed in Sheol as vague shadows of their former selves.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>The books of Isaiah and Daniel allude to the
<b>resurrection</b>, but it wasn't universal, rather it was for those who were
particularly good during their lives on earth.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>The prophet [writers of] Ezekiel coupled the kingdom of God with the
doctrine that persons are rewarded in proportion to their righteousness or
punished in proportion to their sins here on earth.<sup>19</sup><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>A more definite concept of <b>heaven</b>
was offered by the Persian teacher and "Savior" <b>Zoroaster</b>, who
lived about 600 B.C.E.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>His concept was
adopted by one of the Persian trading rivals, the Babylonians.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">569<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">________________________________________________________________<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always">
</span>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family:Arial">In 586 B.C.E. <b>Nebuchadnezzar II</b> took Jerusalem
and forced the Israelites into captivity.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>It was during the two generations in Babylonia that the people of Israel
were exposed to the Babylonian concept of an <b>afterlife</b>â€¦'<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">[382-383].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>'<b><span style="text-transform:
uppercase">Many of the ancient pagan myths, rituals, and even statues were
given a </span></b>"<b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">face lift</span></b>"
<b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">and incorporated into Christianity </span></b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">[newer paganism]<b>.</b></span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">It
was a blatant, and incredibly successful, attempt to preempt the
opposition.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>There were, however, many persons
who would not be taken in by ancient myths or new prevarications.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>These were the seekers of truthâ€”the true
philosophers.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>They were <b>the
descendants of Greek and Roman philosophers who tried to lift humanity from the
darkness of superstition to follow the light of true understanding.</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Through application of science and reason,
these men saw the absurdity of belief in the gods.<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span><b>Lucian of Samosata</b>, for example, wrote satirical dialogues
against religious beliefs and many of the more absurd metaphysical philosophies
of his contemporaries.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>For a time, the descendants of the
rational philosophical tradition were a source of irritation to Christianity,
and the <b>Church Fathers</b> expended a great deal of energy fending off their
attacks.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>With the conversion[overstated]
of <b>Constantine</b>, this annoyance was quickly suppressed.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Wielding the full military power of the
state, the Church outlawed all dissent and ushered in a period of intellectual
suppression unequaled in the history of the world.<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span><b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">For more than a millennium,
any idea contrary to the doctrine of the Church was punishable by torture and
death.</span></b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>If one wishes to
appreciate the intellectual environment during a period of an imposed state
religion, look at the situation in Iran during the 1980s.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>It is no coincidence that in both cases the
wedding of church and state resulted in persecution and suppression.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>In both cases, it was absolutely essential
that all true intellectualism of any kind be snuffed out.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">The
Dark Ages were no accident; they were essential to the establishment of
Christianity.</span></b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>As <b>John
Gardner</b> so graphically wrote in his little masterpiece, <i>Grendel</i>:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>"<b>Theology does not thrive in the
world of action and reaction, change:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>it grows on calm, like the scum on a stagnant pool and it flourishes, it
prospers on decline</b> [attractive expression, but:<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>more complex; does not account for imperialism, etc.]<b>.</b>"<sup>26</sup>'<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[385].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>"<b>In the final analysis all
theology, whether Christian or otherwise, is a marvelous exercise in logic
based on premises that are no more <o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">570<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">________________________________________________________________<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always">
</span>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">verifiableâ€”or
reasonableâ€”than astrology, palmistry, or belief in the Easter Bunny.</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><u>Theology
pretends to search for truth, but no method could lead a person farther away
from the truth than that intellectual charade</u>.<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span><u>The purpose of theology is first and foremost to perpetuate
the religious status quo</u>.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><u>Religion,
in turn, seeks to maintain the social stability necessary for its own
preservation</u>.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>Joseph Campbell
explains:</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>"<b>The paramount
concern of a popular religion cannot be, and never has been</b> '<b>Truth,</b>'
<b>but the maintenance of a certain type of society, the incubation in the
young and refreshment in the old of an approved system of sentiment upon which
the local institutions and government depend.</b>"<sup>27</sup><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>As happens in all great movements
built on a false premise, the seeds of the Church's undoing were sown during
the period of its greatest apparent success.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>Corruption and internal strife demonstrated that the Church hierarchy was
no more godlike than any temporal institution.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>At the same time, the European aristocracy became concerned about its
own erosion of power.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Churches are
supposed to support the state and vice-versa; when either seeks to usurp the
powers of the other a mortal conflict will ensue.<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>And it oftentimes did.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>A
similar sequence of events could be traced in most of the other major world
religions.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>The greatest blow to Christianity
came with the invention of the most liberating tool in human historyâ€”<b>Johann
Gutenberg</b>'s [c. 1398 â€“ 1468] printing press [and, the Internet?].<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Despite the fact that <b>Gutenberg's first
publication was the Bible</b>, the more perceptive clerics realized that the
printing press was a grave threat to the Church's dominion over the human mind and
sought to have it destroyed.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>Unfortunately for the Church, others thought that it could be
effectively controlled and utilized to the Church's advantage.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Although, as <b>Galileo</b> [1564 â€“ 1642]
and many others were to discover, <b>the Church would never abandon the fight
to retain control of the human mind</b>, in the end the Church gradually lost
ground."<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[386-387].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">'<b>17<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">Why the Myths Live On:<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">Today's Psychological Motivators<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">What the populace learned to believe without reasons,
who could refute it then by means of reasons?<span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><b>â€”Friedrich
Nietzsche</b> [1844 â€“ 1900]<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="right" style="text-align:right;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">It
would be tempting but overly simplistic to say that people flock to churches to
be reassured that God does exist and all the promises of the Bible, especially
an <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">571<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">________________________________________________________________<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always">
</span>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">afterlife,
will come true.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>But this is only part
of the story.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>Erich Fromm</b> [1900
â€“ 1980] wrote:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>The influence of any
doctrine or idea depends on the extent to which it appeals to psychic needs in
the character of those whom it addresses.</b><sup>1</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>Shakespeare </b>[1564 â€“ 1616]<b> </b>expressed
this idea more poetically in his play <i>Henry IV</i>:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>"<b>The wish is father to the thought.</b>"<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>The purpose of this chapter is to analyze
the psychological needs religion fills.<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>The philosopher <b>David Hume</b>
[1711 â€“ 1776] began to investigate some psychological aspects of belief in his <b><i>Dialogues
Concerning Natural Religion</i></b> (1779), but <b>Ludwig Feuerbach</b> [1804 â€“
1872] <b>was the first to fully explore the psychological basis of
Christianity.</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>In 1841 <b>Feuerbach</b>
published his classic work, <b><i>The Essence of Christianity</i></b>.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Although he explicitly examines
Christianity, his psychological analysis could be extended to any
religion.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>Feuerbach postulated that
God was no more than</b> "the realized wish of the heart, the wish exalted
to the certainty of its fulfillment, of its reality, to that undoubting
certainty before which no contradiction of the understanding, no difficulty of
experience or of the external world, maintains its ground."<sup>72</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>According to Feuerbach, the attributes of
God are simply a projection of human needs, hopes and longings:</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>a being who is all-good, all-powerful,
all-wise, all-happiness and, most of all, eternal.'<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>[389].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>'Ultimately, belief in God may be a
genetically determined characteristic of human beings.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>Sociobiologist Edward O. Wilson</b> [born
1929]<b> thinks that belief in God is a coping mechanism, fundamental to the
very nature of our species:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span></b>"Beliefs
are really enabling mechanisms for survival.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span><b>Religions, like other human institutions, evolve so as to enhance the
persistence and influence of their practitioners.</b>"<sup>6</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>If <b>Wilson</b> is correct, as long as
society fails to meet the psychological needs discussed below with more
successful means, we might expect the belief in theism to continue.'<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[390].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">'<b>The
Universal Desire for Immortality<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">John
Steinbeck</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial"> [1902 â€“ 1968] <b>wrote:<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">After the bare requisites to living and reproducing,
man wants most to leave some record of himself, a proof, perhaps, that he
really existed.</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>He leaves his proof on wood, or stone, or on
the lives of other people.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>This deep
desire exists in everyone, from the boy who writes dirty words in the public
toilet to the Buddha who etches his image in the race mind.<sup>7<o:p></o:p></sup></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><sup><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></sup></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><sup><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></sup></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">572<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">________________________________________________________________<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;

</span>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family:Arial">No doubt such a desire drives me to write this book
[and me (LS)â€”this website].<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>However,
for most people, simply leaving an artifact behind is not enough.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>They can't bear the thought of leaving this
life in the first place</b> [describes me (LS)].<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>Based upon their own analysis and a review of other studies, [<b>Michael</b>]
<b>Argyle</b> and [<b>Benjamin</b>] <b>Beit-Hallahmi</b> conclude that
"this group of studies provides very strong support for the theory that <b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">fear of death</span></b> [see
christianism.com, 2939-3058] <b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">is the
basis for religious beliefs.</span></b>"<sup>8</sup><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>To say that most people believe in
some sort of god is only to recognize that virtually all people would like to
escape death.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>I agree with <b>Schopenhauer
</b>[1788 â€“ 1860] that the fundamental purpose of religion, and hence the
belief in God, is a desperate effort to escape mortality.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>"<b>For if one could establish their
doctrine of immortality for them in some other way, the lively zeal for their
gods would at once cool, and it would give place to complete indifference.</b>"<sup>9</sup>'<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[391].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>'<b>To make their adherents desirous
of immortality, Christianity had to keep them focused on the inevitability and
proximity of death.</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>The Christian
funeral service does an excellent job of pressing upon the mind the imminence
of death by reminding the living how temporal and fleeting is their stay here
on earth.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>They are told not to worry
though, because this life is simply a "vale of tears."<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>So be happy at the thought of impending
death because it is "only through dying that one can gain eternal
life."<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>The entire ceremony is an
apology for living.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Living for its part
is virtually an evil for which one must atone by dying.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Christian prayers for the dead contain no
reference to how sweet life can be or may have been to the deceased.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>How much more life-affirming was the
Native American philosophy that looked upon life as good and death as simply a
natural event in nature's cycle of death and rebirth.</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">The
Epicurean philosophyâ€”so often distorted by Christian theologiansâ€”also offered a
positive outlook encouraging people to enjoy the feast of life and then
graciously depart the banquet to make room for others.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">Death
is the very mother's milk of religion.</span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>During the Middle Ages, the plague sent thousands of poor,
frightened people flocking to the churches.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>In this century, war and the threat of it have been major boons to
religion.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>It is not surprising, then,
that after the horrors of World War I, one Christian writer expressed a view
undoubtedly shared by many others:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>"If, even for a few generations, we act on our own conjecture of <b>immortality</b>,
the larger vision, the more profound basis of purpose, will so advance human
existence as to make this war worth its price."<sup>10</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>What he is really saying is that the growth
in <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">religious
fervor following a war is worth the horror and death.<span style="mso-spacerun:

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><b>If death is the ultimate
incentive for religion, pleasure is the ultimate disincentive.</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>To make this life pleasurable distracts our
focus from death and the desire for <b>immortality</b>.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Consequently, the need for religion is
weakened.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Therefore, religions present
pain as "purifying" and suffering as "ennobling."<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Pleasure is equated with selfishness as if
it were a contradiction of logic to state that an individual might seek both
personal pleasure and the pleasure of others as well.<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>However, no such contradiction need exist if we recognize that

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>In its effort to abrogate the joy

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">'<b>The
prospect of physical death is central to a brilliant marketing strategy

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>'<b>For many people religious

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Frequently, joining a religious

now regularly sponsor dances and social events to draw the lonely ones into

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>The psychological feeling of a

offers a small buffer from life's many bad knocks.<span style="mso-spacerun:

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>The desire for security in a world
fraught with change and uncertainty may result in a people seeking a
paternalistic, caring god to protect and shelter them against the vicissitudes

one woman who frankly admitted that in her mind God was synonymous with her

may be there.<sup>15</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>In a sense,
it is a case of arrested development.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;

once filled by their earthly parents, are now satisfied by their imaginary

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>'<b>Feuerbach </b>[Ludwig Feuerbach

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">"<b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">Faith gives man a peculiar sense of his own

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">________________________________________________________________<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always">
</span>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">'<b>Escape
from Responsibility<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">This
all leads to my next point:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>although
Western religions rely heavily on guilt to keep their followers in line, belief
in God is oftentimes used by believers as an escape from acceptance of personal
responsibility both for one's own destiny and, more so, for the fate of
others.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Even when the believers' world
is crumbling around them due to their own mistakes, they can be comforted,
secure in the knowledge that it is "God's will."<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>As Schopenhauer</b> [1788 â€“ 1860] <b>pointed
out, </b>"<b>it is far more endurable to have our misfortune brought
clearly before us than our incapacity.</b>"<sup>28</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>I recall a friend's reaction when he went
bankrupt.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>A true believer in the most
radical sense, he simply concluded that this was either God's way of punishing
him for some past sin, or a way of testing him, just as Job was tested.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>In either case, it was God's will and
clearly not due to incompetence on his part.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>I marveled that he never lost five minutes of sleep over the
situation.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Indeed religion is a
wonderful, although terribly addictive, drug.'<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>[400].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">"<b>The
Free Lunch Syndrome<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">Most
people want very much to believe there is someone who will give them something
just for the asking.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">E.
Haldeman-Julius</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial"> [1889 â€“ 1951] <b>recognized
<span style="text-transform:uppercase">the psychological similarity between the
idea of God and that of Santa Claus</span>,</b><sup>30</sup> <b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">Santa Claus being an infantile notion of God</span></b>â€¦."<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[401].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">'<b>The
Need for Peer and Parental Approval<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">One
of the great American myths is the stereotypical rugged individualist.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>The truth is that <b>most Americans</b>,
like all other people, <b>are scared to death of individuality.</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Psychologist <b>Eric Fromm </b>[1900 â€“ 1980]<b>
observed:</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>"<b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">Man is, by origin, a herd animal.</span></b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>His actions are determined by an instinctive
impulse to follow the leaders and to have close contact with the other animals
around him."<sup>31</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>Elsewhere, <b>Fromm</b> makes the chilling observation:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">"<b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">There is nothing inhuman, evil or irrational
which does not give some comfort provided it is shared by a group.</span></b>"<sup>32</sup>'<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[402].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>'<b>It is a sad fact that most
people's lives are primarily characterized by boredom and drudgery.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Lacking an appreciation of music, art,
literature, or even an entertaining hobby, they seek escape through the exotic
and/or <o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">576<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">________________________________________________________________<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always">
</span>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">occult.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span></span></b><u><span style="font-family:Arial">Religion
fills the bill nicely</span></u><span style="font-family:Arial">.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><u>It's small wonder, then, that no matter
how inherently contradictory or downright absurd a religious dogma is, it
remains a cherished belief for most members of society</u>.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>In fact, <b>in Schopenhauer's opinion,</b>
"<b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">some absolute contradictions,
some actual absurdities, are an essential ingredient in a complete religion</span>,</b>"<sup>44</sup>
<b>since they give the appearance of greater profundity to most men.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>M.D. Goulder correctly observed that</b> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">"<b><span style="text-transform:uppercase">when we remove the mist we remove the mystery</span>.</b>"<sup>45</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">Moreover,
since people are told that by its very nature religion is incomprehensible to
the ordinary mind, they can rationalize why it doesn't appear to make any
sense.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>The mysteries can be left to the
priests who, since they allegedly speak for God, can provide explanations for
the masses by means of simple, albeit meaningless, allegories.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Or people can opt out, completely
suppressing all attempts at reason in favor of mysticism, and seek to "experience"
God directly.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>In any case, <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial;
text-transform:uppercase">religion performs the same function as all the other
forms of psychic entertainmentâ€”escape from reality.</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial">'<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[407].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>'<b>Schopenhauer recognized that</b>
"priestsâ€¦must impart their metaphysical dogmas to man at a very early age,
before judgment has awakened from its morning slumber, thus in early childhood,
for then every well-impressed dogma, however senseless it may be, remains
forever."<sup>48</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Echoing
this sentiment, <b>Charles Darwin</b> [1809 â€“ 1882] might have had a
forethought of the bitter opposition his theories would face from religious
leaders when he wrote that:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">â€¦<b>the constant inculcation in a belief in God on
the minds of children [produces] so strong an effectâ€¦that it would be as
difficult for them to throw off their belief in God as a monkey to throw off
its instinctive fear and hatred of a snake.</b><sup>49</sup><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>It is this desire for indoctrination
that is behind the efforts of proponents of prayer in the classroom.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Prayer in itself isn't the issue, since
children can pray to their heart's content at home.<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>What they seek is official support for prayer to pressure all
children into accepting theism and, ultimately, <b>Christianity</b>.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Even a "moment of silence" would
have the law of the land giving tacit support for theism.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Given the implicit endorsement of the
federal government to the concept of prayer, which obviously implies a god,
children will have an enormous incentiveâ€”perhaps pressure is a better wordâ€”to
believe.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>"<b>The law of imitation
operates and nonconformity is not an outstanding characteristic of <o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">577<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">________________________________________________________________<o:p></o:p></span></p>

</span>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">children.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>The result is an obvious pressure upon
children to attend.</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial">"<sup>50</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>With these words, <b>Justice Felix
Frankfurter</b> [1882 â€“ 1965] recognized the true intent of the effort to
introduce prayer into the schools.'<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>[408-409].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>"<b>To sum up, it should by now
be quite apparent that, in part, religion grew out of a need by early humans to
explain and control the mysterious workings of nature.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>However, the psychological needs and fears
that theism and religious organizations exploit provide an even greater
motivation to religious belief.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>These
include:<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.25in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:.5in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;

</span></span><!--[endif]--><b><span style="font-family:Arial">the universal desire
to escape death </span></b><span style="font-family:Arial">[see
christianism.com, 2939-3058];<b><o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.25in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:.5in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial">â€”<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">the need for identity
and status (a sense of belonging to a group);<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:1.25in;text-indent:-1.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:list .25in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;

</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">the need on the part of
certain individuals (priests and ministers) to exercise <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="text-indent:.25in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">power over others and secure a lucrative livelihood;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.25in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:.5in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial">â€”<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">the need for security
in a world of increasing uncertainty;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.25in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:.5in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial">â€”<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">the desire for justice
and / or revenge, in this world or in the hereafter;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.25in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:.5in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial">â€”<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">the inability to accept
responsibility for one's errors;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:1.25in;text-indent:-1.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;

mso-bidi-font-family:Arial">â€”<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">the desire for a reward
to make up for present suffering;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:1.25in;text-indent:-1.25in;tab-stops:
