<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:1.25in;text-indent:-1.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:decimal .25in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial">â€”<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">the desire to get
something by merely wishing for it;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;tab-stops:list .25in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.25in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:list .25in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial">â€”<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">the need for peer and
parental approval coupled with the fear of social ostracism for not believing;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:1.25in;text-indent:-1.25in;tab-stops:
list .25in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:1.25in;text-indent:-1.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:list .25in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial">â€”<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">the unwillingness or
inability of people to break out of their ignorance;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:1.25in;text-indent:-1.25in;tab-stops:
list .25in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:1.25in;text-indent:-1.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:list .25in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial">â€”<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">the entertainment value
of believing in the occult; and<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:1.25in;text-indent:-1.25in;tab-stops:
list .25in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:1.25in;text-indent:-1.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo6;
tab-stops:list .25in"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family:&quot;Wingdings 2&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial">â€”<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="font-family:Arial">intellectual
conditioning by organized religion.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="text-indent:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">Rationalist <b>Gordon Stein </b>[1941 â€“ 1996] offers
a similar list of psychological motivations for believers.<sup>53</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>Argyle</b> lists seven psychological
roots of religious belief:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>parent
figure, conflict anxiety, need resolution, identity development, solving
intellectual problems (recall the need to explain discussed in the last
chapter), and biochemical processes (such [as] <b>Wilson</b>'s sociobiology <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="text-indent:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="text-indent:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">578<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">________________________________________________________________<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always">
</span>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">theory).<sup>54</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>Brown</b> adds two more:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>social learning and external locus of
control.<sup>55</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>As you can see,
these lists approximate my own."<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>[410].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="text-indent:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="text-indent:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="text-indent:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">'Most people are familiar with <b>Marx</b>'s
statement which referred to <b>religion </b>as the <b>opium of the people</b>.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>However, he is usually quoted out of context
and the real significance of his observation is lost.<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span><b>Marx </b>[Karl Marx 1818 â€“ 1883]<b> wrote:<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="text-indent:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">[Karl Marx] <b>Man makes religion:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>religion does not make man.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Religion is indeed man's self-consciousness
and self-awareness so long as he has not found himself or has lost himself
againâ€¦.Religion is the sigh of the oppressed creature, the sentiment of a
heartless world and the soul of soulless conditions.<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span></b>It [<b><u>Religion</u></b><u>] <b>is the opium of the people</b></u><b>
</b>[from a professor of Karl Marx, Bruno Bauer (see christianism.com, 107,
130, 416)]<b>â€¦.Religion is only the illusory sun about which man revolves so
long as he does not revolve around himself.</b><sup>59</sup><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="text-indent:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">It
was, therefore, <b>Marx</b>'s view that for people to give up the illusions
which comprise religious belief would first require that society alter the
conditions requiring the illusion.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>For
"it is not the consciousness of men which determines their existence but
on the contrary, their social condition which determines their
consciousness."<sup>60</sup><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span>Actually, as we have found out since the time of <b>Marx</b>,
consciousness and existence are interactive and, as such, religious belief is
even more fundamental to man's psychological makeup than <b>Marx</b>
supposed.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>But <b>Marx, like Hume and
Feuerbach,</b> correctly <b>recognized that humans create an image of God to
meet their specific needs.</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>When
needs change, the idealization of God changes.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span><b>Albert Schweitzer</b> [1875 â€“ 1965] argued [<b>stated</b>] <b>that
each period of history recreated Jesus in accordance with its own character.</b><sup>61</sup>'<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[411].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">"<b>19<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">Conclusion</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial">"<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[439]<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>'<b>Not only is there no evidence
for the existence of a god or gods </b>[<b>or goddess or goddesses</b>] but the
classic definition of God is fraught with contradictions that would make the
existence of such a being as impossible as a square circle.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>After thousands of years of using the term
"God," and the sacrifice of millions of lives to support one
conception of the term over another, we humans are still no closer to providing
a meaningful definition.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">579<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">________________________________________________________________<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA"><br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always">
</span>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial">It is not difficult to trace the origins of myths
concerning the gods. </span></b><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</span>Early man needed a simple explanation for the
mysteries of nature.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Positing a being
with human qualities not only explained the capriciousness of nature but
offered primitive peoples the opportunity of swaying the intentions of the gods
and, hence, the opportunity of controlling nature.<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>It is equally easy to understand the <b>psychological motivations</b>
which refined the myths and continue to sustain them today.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>People will always fear death, attempt to
rationalize their hostility to others, and seek to escape loneliness.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>Belief in God and religious affiliation
fills these needs.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>There are also
potential penalties for opposing such beliefs, such as social ostracism.<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>While the promoters of theism have
powerful motivators, both psychological and monetary, to assist them, <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial;
text-transform:uppercase">there is no profit to be made by promoting nontheism.</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">It's
like forming a society of those who have neither seen nor believe in UFOs.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><u><span style="font-family:Arial;
text-transform:uppercase">Few people care passionately about what they don't believe</span></u></b><b><span style="font-family:Arial;text-transform:uppercase">.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>On balance, theism is neither
beneficial nor even neutral to human beings.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;
</span><b>Like a placebo, theism can effect cures.</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>It can also act as a drug to alleviate the
pain associated with existence.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><b>But
in the long run it is an addiction that slows our efforts to understand human
nature and hampers progress toward universal peace and happiness</b>â€¦.'<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[441].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><span style="mso-tab-count:1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>"<b>In a 1992 lecture</b> to
the National Planning Forum, former U.S. Secretary of State <b>Henry Kissinger</b>
[born 1923] <b>stated that following the fall of the Soviet Union one of the
primary roles for the United States was to prevent Moslem fundamentalism from
becoming the dominant force in Asia.</b><sup>1</sup><span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>His focus was to narrow:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial;
text-transform:uppercase">fundamentalism anywhere in the world is a threat to
peace.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>In the United States, Christian
fundamentalism is the most serious threat to our freedom and social progress.</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial">"<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[442].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">580<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">________________________________________________________________<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="text-indent:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">'<b>I close with the words of a man who has written
two sentences that have strongly touched my life.<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp; </span>His name is David Tribe</b> [born 1931] and, after studying the
legacy of <b>freethinkers</b> of the past in terms of such social advances as
free, secular, and compulsory education; family planning; the role of women,
and the like, he wrote:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial">[David Tribe (one of my (LS) favorites)] <b>The
influence of Freethinkers</b> is not to be seen in the numbers that have joined
their organization or stood up on the fringe to be countedâ€¦<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><b><span style="font-family:Arial">It is the way people's</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial"> vital secondary [<b>personal</b>] <b>beliefs have
been affected</b>, <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left:.5in;tab-stops:.5in"><u><span style="font-family:Arial">whatever their views of ultimate reality</span></u><span style="font-family:Arial">, <u>whether they stay inside or leave the churches</u>.<sup>3</sup>'<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[443] [end of text].<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoFooter" align="center" style="text-align:center;tab-stops:.5in center 3.0in right 6.0in"><span style="font-family:Arial"><!--[if !supportEmptyParas]-->&nbsp;<!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></span></p>
